//var ITO4T_URL = "/wcsstore/FastShopSAS/ITO4T_timer.txt";
  // Set this to the same value as WRM_ANALYZER_QUEUE_WAIT
  // on the Web Response Time monitoring agent.
  var ITO4T_WAIT = 60000;
   
  var ITO4T_start_query = "brt";
  var ITO4T_end_query   = "crt";

  function sendITO4TPageTag(query)
  {
    try
    {
      var ITO4T_req = window.XMLHttpRequest ?
                        new XMLHttpRequest() :
                        new ActiveXObject("MSXML2.XMLHTTP.3.0");
      ITO4T_req.open("GET", ITO4T_URL + "?" + query, true);
      ITO4T_req.setRequestHeader("If-Modified-Since",
      "Thu, 1 Jan 1970 00:00:01 GMT");
      ITO4T_req.send(null);
    }
    catch(err) {}
  }
  
  // send starting page tag immediately
  sendITO4TPageTag(ITO4T_start_query);
  
  // callback to send the closing page tag
  // (with calculated client rendering time)
  var ITO4T_timeout = false;
  var ITO4T_done    = false;

  function getITO4TRenderTime()
  {
    if (! ITO4T_done)
    {
      var ITO4T_now = new Date();
      var ITO4T_render_time = ITO4T_now - ITO4T_start_time;
      sendITO4TPageTag(ITO4T_end_query + "=" + ITO4T_render_time);
      
      ITO4T_done = true;
      if (ITO4T_timeout)
      {
        clearTimeout(ITO4T_timeout);
      }
    }
  }
  
  // invoke getITO4TRenderTime() if we time out
  // before body.onload or .onunload is called.
  ITO4T_timeout = setTimeout("getITO4TRenderTime()", ITO4T_WAIT);

	//Summary: Returns the absolute URL to use for prefixing any Ajax URL call.
	//Description: Dojo does not handle the case where the parameters in the URL are delimeted by the "/" forward slash. Therefore, in order to
	//             workaround the issue, all AJAX requests must be done using absolute URLs rather than relative.
	//Returns: The absolute URL to use for prefixing any Ajax URL call.
	function getAbsoluteURL() {
		if (absoluteURL != "") {
			var currentURL = document.URL;
			var currentProtocol = "";
		
			if (currentURL.indexOf("://") != -1) {
				currentProtocol = currentURL.substring(0, currentURL.indexOf("://"));
			}
			
			var savedProtocol = "";
			if (absoluteURL.indexOf("://") != -1) {
				savedProtocol = absoluteURL.substring(0, absoluteURL.indexOf("://"));
			}
			
			if (currentProtocol != savedProtocol) {
				absoluteURL = currentProtocol + absoluteURL.substring(absoluteURL.indexOf("://"));
			}
		}
		
		return absoluteURL;
	}
	//Summary: Returns the path pointing to the shared image directory.
	//Description: In order to get the image directory path in any javascript file, this function can be used.
	//Returns: The path to reference images.
	function getImageDirectoryPath() {
		return imageDirectoryPath;
	}
	//Summary: Returns the path pointing to the directory containing color-dependant image files.
	//Description: In order to get the directory containing color-dependant image files in any javascript file, this function can be used.
	//Returns: The path to reference color-dependant image files.
	function getStyleDirectoryPath() {
		return styleDirectoryPath;
	}

<script type="text/javascript">
/* Number.prototype.format(n, x, s, c)
 * 
 * @param integer n: length of decimal
 * @param integer x: length of whole part
 * @param mixed   s: sections delimiter
 * @param mixed   c: decimal delimiter
 */
Number.prototype.format = function(n, x, s, c) {
    var re = '\\d(?=(\\d{' + (x || 3) + '})+' + (n > 0 ? '\\D' : '$') + ')',
        num = this.toFixed(Math.max(0, ~~n));

    return (c ? num.replace('.', c) : num).replace(new RegExp(re, 'g'), '$&' + (s || ','));
};
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
function loadBazaarVoice(){
	
		var partNumbers = [];
		partNumber = document.getElementsByName("bazaarVoicePartNumber");
		if(partNumber.length > 0){
			for(i=0; i<partNumber.length;i++){
				productIds.push(partNumber[i].value);
			}
			$BV.ui( 'rr', 'inline_ratings', {'productIds' : productIds , containerPrefix : 'BVRRInlineRating'});
		}
	
}
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
	
	function getGenderLabel(gender) {
		var labelMale = 'Masculino';
		var labelFemale = 'Feminino';
		
		var label = "";
		
		if (gender) {
			if (gender == 'Female') {
				label = labelFemale;
			} else if (gender == 'Male') {
				label = labelMale;
			}
		}
		
		return label;
	}
</script>

	<script type="text/javascript">
	
		function getGTMGenderLabel(gender) {
			var labelMale = "M";
			var labelFemale = "F";
			
			var label = "";
			
			if (gender) {
				if (gender == 'Female') {
					label = labelFemale;
				} else if (gender == 'Male') {
					label = labelMale;
				}
			}
			
			return label;
		}
	</script>

<script type="text/javascript">

dojo.addOnLoad(function() {
	if(document.getElementById("widget_departments")){
		document.getElementById("widget_departments").style.display = "block";
	}
	if(DepartmentJS.requestFromHome == 'true'){
		document.getElementById("drop_down").style.display = "block";
	} else {
		document.getElementById("drop_down").style.display = "none";
	}
	DepartmentJS.init(DepartmentJS.requestFromHome);
	
	wc.render.getRefreshControllerById("DepartmentDropdownController").url = "/webapp/wcs/stores/servlet/DepartmentDropdownView?storeId=10151&catalogId=11052&langId=-6&hotsite=fastshop&isFirstRefresh=true";
	
	DepartmentJS.initializeCatNodes();  
	dojo.query("div#widget_departments > .drop_down > .middle > .left_border > .right_border > .departments > .department").forEach(function(node){
		dojo.connect(node, "onfocus", DepartmentJS, dojo.partial(DepartmentJS._onDepartmentFocus, node));
		dojo.connect(node, "onmouseover", DepartmentJS, dojo.partial(DepartmentJS._onDepartmentFocus, node));
		dojo.connect(node, "onblur", DepartmentJS, dojo.partial(DepartmentJS._onDepartmentNoFocus, node));
		if(dojo.isIE){
			dojo.connect(node, "onmouseleave", DepartmentJS, dojo.partial(DepartmentJS._onDepartmentNoFocus, node));
		}
		else{
			dojo.connect(node, "onmouseout", DepartmentJS, dojo.partial(DepartmentJS._onDepartmentNoFocus, node));
		}			
	});
   	dojo.query('#widget_departments a').forEach(function(node){
	   dojo.connect(node, 'onclick', function(){isFastShopLink=true});
   	});
});

dojo.addOnUnload(function() {
	if(document.getElementById("drop_down") && DepartmentJS.requestFromHome != 'true'){
		document.getElementById("drop_down").style.display = "none";
	}
});

</script>

		wc.service.declare({
			id: "AjaxSearchAddressByZipCode",
			actionId: "FastShopSearchAddress",
			url: getAbsoluteURL() + "FastShopSearchAddress",
			successHandler: function(serviceResponse) {
				MessageHelper.hideAndClearMessage();
				cursor_clear();
				var streetName = serviceResponse.searchAddessResult.address.streetName;
				var neighborhood = serviceResponse.searchAddessResult.address.district;
				var city = serviceResponse.searchAddessResult.address.city;
				var state = serviceResponse.searchAddessResult.address.state.literal;
				var streetType = dojo.string.trim(serviceResponse.searchAddessResult.address.streetType);
				var address = dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_address1_1");
				var neighborHoodField = dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_address2_3");
				var streetTypeField = dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_streetType_1");
				var streetTypeTempField = dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_streetTypeTemp_1");
				var stateTempField = dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_stateTemp_1");
				var number = dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_address2_1");
				var addressExt = dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_address2_2");
				
				if (streetName.length > address.maxLength) {
					streetName = "";
				}
				if (neighborhood.length > neighborHoodField.maxLength) {
					neighborhood = "";
				}

				address.value = streetName;
				neighborHoodField.value = neighborhood;
				dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_city_1").value = city;
				dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_stateTemp_1").value = state;
				dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_state_1").value = state;
				streetTypeTempField.value = streetType;
				streetTypeField.value = streetType;
				
				if(streetTypeTempField.value == "") {
					streetTypeTempField.disabled = false;
					dojo.removeClass(streetTypeTempField, 'ronly');
				}else {
					streetTypeTempField.disabled= "disabled";
					dojo.addClass(streetTypeTempField, 'ronly');
				}
				
				if (streetName == "") {
					address.readOnly = false;
					dojo.removeClass(address, 'ronly');
					dojo.removeAttr(address, 'tabIndex');
					
					if (neighborhood == "") {
						neighborHoodField.readOnly = false;
						dojo.removeClass(neighborHoodField, 'ronly');
						dojo.removeAttr(neighborHoodField, 'tabIndex');
					}
				} else {
					address.readOnly = "readonly";
					neighborHoodField.readOnly = "readonly";
	
					dojo.addClass(address, 'ronly');

					if (neighborhood == "") {
						neighborHoodField.readOnly = false;
						dojo.removeClass(neighborHoodField, 'ronly');
						dojo.removeAttr(neighborHoodField, 'tabIndex');
					} else {
						dojo.addClass(neighborHoodField, 'ronly');
					}

					stateTempField.disabled = "disabled";
				}			
					
				number.readOnly = false;
				dojo.removeClass(number, 'ronly');
				addressExt.readOnly = false;
				dojo.removeClass(addressExt, 'ronly');	
			},
			failureHandler: function(serviceResponse) {
				if (serviceResponse.errorMessage) {
					MessageHelper.displayErrorMessage(serviceResponse.errorMessage);
			  	} else {
					if (serviceResponse.errorMessageKey) {
						MessageHelper.displayErrorMessage(serviceResponse.errorMessageKey);
					}
			  	}
			  	cursor_clear();
			  	
			  	var addressField = dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_address1_1");
				var neighborHoodField = dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_address2_3");
				var streetTypeField = dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_streetType_1");
				var streetTypeTempField = dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_streetTypeTemp_1");
				var number = dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_address2_1");
				var addressExt = dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_address2_2");
				var stateTempField = dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_stateTemp_1");
				var cityField = dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_city_1");
			  	
			  	if (serviceResponse.exceptionData && serviceResponse.exceptionData.errorCode && (serviceResponse.exceptionData.errorCode == "1" || serviceResponse.exceptionData.errorCode == "2")) {
			  		addressField.readOnly = true;
					neighborHoodField.readOnly = true;
					cityField.readOnly = true;
					stateTempField.disabled = "disabled";
					stateTempField.readOnly = true;
					dojo.addClass(stateTempField, "ronly");
			  	} else {
			  		addressField.readOnly = false;
					neighborHoodField.readOnly = false;
					cityField.readOnly = false;
					stateTempField.disabled = "";
					stateTempField.readOnly = false;
					dojo.removeClass(stateTempField, "ronly");
			  	}
			}
		});
	});
	
	function clearFieldNumberCompl(){
		dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_address2_1").value = "";
		dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_address2_2").value = "";
	}
		
	function populateAddressFields(data) {
		dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_zipCode_1").value = data.zIPCode;
		dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_address1_1").value = data.streetName;
		dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_address2_3").value = data.district;
		dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_city_1").value = data.city;
		dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_stateTemp_1").value = data.state.literal;
		dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_state_1").value = data.state.literal;
		dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_streetTypeTemp_1").value = dojo.string.trim(data.streetType);
		dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_streetType_1").value = dojo.string.trim(data.streetType);
	}

	function searchAddress() {
		var zipCode = dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_zipCode_1").value;
		
		if (zipCode && zipCode != "") {
			dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_address1_1").value = "";
			dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_address2_3").value = "";
			dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_city_1").value = "";
			dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_stateTemp_1").value = "";
			dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_state_1").value = "";
			dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_streetTypeTemp_1").value = "";
			dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_streetType_1").value = "";
			
			dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_address1_1").readOnly = true;
			dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_address2_3").readOnly = true;
			dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_city_1").readOnly = true;
			dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_stateTemp_1").disabled = "disabled";
			dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_streetTypeTemp_1").disabled = "disabled";
			
			dojo.addClass(dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_address1_1"), "ronly");
			dojo.addClass(dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_address2_3"), "ronly");
			dojo.addClass(dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_city_1"), "ronly");
			dojo.addClass(dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_stateTemp_1"), "ronly");
			dojo.addClass(dojo.byId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_streetTypeTemp_1"), "ronly");
			
			if ((zipCode.indexOf('-') == '-1' && zipCode.length == 8) || (zipCode.indexOf('-') != '-1' && zipCode.length == 9)) {
				var params = {};
				params["searchBy"] = "searchByZipCode";
				params["zipCode"] = zipCode;
				params["storeId"] = WCParamJS.storeId;
				params["catalogId"] = WCParamJS.catalogId;
				params["langId"] = WCParamJS.langId;
				params["hotsite"] = WCParamJS.hotsite;
				setCurrentId("WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_zipCode_1"); 
				submitRequest(); 
				cursor_wait(); 
				wc.service.invoke('AjaxSearchAddressByZipCode', params);
			}
		}
	}
	
	function maskCEP(e, obj) {
		restrict('num', '', e);
		maskedInput(e, 'cep', obj);
	}
	
	function validarCaracteresCEP(c){
		somenteNumerosCEP(c);
	}
	
	//nome
	function validarCaracteresNome(c){
		somenteLetras(c);
	}
	
	//numero,complemento e rg
	function validarNumerosELetras(c){
		somenteNumeroELetras(c);
	}
	
</script>

    <script type="text/javascript">
    function validateSMS($elm){
		var $celphone = dojo.byId('WC_PersonalInfoExtension_mobile_div_12'),
			msg = 'Para receber informações e promoções via SMS, é necessário preencher um número de celular válido';
		
		if( $elm.checked ){
			ValidateForm.validationMethods.required($celphone, true, msg);
		}
	}
    
    dojo.addOnLoad(function() {
        dojo.query('#WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_links_1').onclick(function(e){
            dojo.stopEvent(e);

            ValidateForm.submitHandler = function(){
                var form = document.Register;

                //set value for lastName fields
                //form.lastName.value = form.firstName.value;
                
                if ('UserRegistrationAddForm' == 'UserRegistrationUpdateForm') {
					if(form.logonPassword_old.name == "logonPassword")
					{
						
						form.logonPassword_old.name = "logonPassword_old";
						form.logonPasswordVerify_old.name = "logonPasswordVerify_old";
					}
					/*check whether the values in password and verify password fields match, if so, update the password. */ 
					if (form.logonPassword_old.value.length != 0)
					{
						if(form.logonPassword_old.value!= form.logonPasswordVerify_old.value)
						{
							ValidateForm.showError(form.logonPasswordVerify_old, 'O Campo confirmação de senha está diferente do campo senha.')
							//MessageHelper.formErrorHandleClient(form.logonPasswordVerify_old.id,MessageHelper.messages["PWDREENTER_DO_NOT_MATCH"]);
							return ; 
						}
						form.logonPassword_old.name = "logonPassword";
						form.logonPasswordVerify_old.name = "logonPasswordVerify";
					} 
                }
			


                /* Checks whether the customer has registered for promotional e-mails. */
                if(form.sendMeEmail && form.sendMeEmail.checked){
                    form.receiveEmail.value = true;
                }
                else {
                    form.receiveEmail.value = false;
                }
                
                if(form.sendMeSMSNotification &&  form.sendMeSMSNotification.checked){
                    form.receiveSMSNotification.value = true;
                }
                else {
                    form.receiveSMSNotification.value = false;
                }
                
                if(form.sendMeSMSPreference && form.sendMeSMSPreference.checked){
                    form.receiveSMS.value = true;
                }
                else {
                    form.receiveSMS.value = false;
                }
                
                if(form.sendMeSMSPreference2 && form.sendMeSMSPreference2.checked){
                    form.receiveSMS2.value = true;
                }
                else {
                    form.receiveSMS2.value = false;
                }
                
                if(form.sendMePartnerEmailPreference && form.sendMePartnerEmailPreference.checked){
                    form.receivePartnerEmail.value = true;
                }
                else {
                    form.receivePartnerEmail.value = false;
                }                
                
                if(form.mobileDeviceEnabled != null && form.mobileDeviceEnabled.value == "true"){
                    if(!MyAccountDisplay.validateMobileDevice(form)){
                        return;
                    }
                }
                if(form.birthdayEnabled != null && form.birthdayEnabled.value == "true"){
                    if(!MyAccountDisplay.validateBirthday(form)){
                        return;
                    }
                }
                /* For Handling multiple clicks. */
                if(!submitRequest()){
                    return;
                }

                form.state.value = form.stateTemp.value;
                form.streetType.value = form.streetTypeTemp.value;

                if(WCParamJS.hotsite != "televendas"){
                   	form.submit();
                }
                else{
                    if(telesalesJS.isSellerRegisteringUser){
                    	telesalesJS.requestSellerPassword();
                    }
                    else{
                    	form.submit();
                    }
                }
            }

            ValidateForm.validate({
                form : dojo.byId('Register'),

                rules : {
                    
                            //nome
                            'WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_NameEntryForm_FormInput_firstName_1': {
                                required : true,
                                minlen : 2,
                                mincomp : [' ',2]
                            },
                            //cep
                            'WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_zipCode_1': {
                                required : true,
                                equalLen : 9
                            },
                        
                    //logradouro
                    'WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_streetTypeTemp_1' : {
                        required : true
                    },

                    //endereco
                    'WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_address1_1' : {
                        required : true
                    },

                    //numero
                    'WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_address2_1' : {
                        required : true
                    },

                    //bairro
                    'WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_address2_3' : {
                        required : true
                    },

                    //moradia
                    'WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_houseType_1' : {
                        required : true
                    },

                    //estado
                    'WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_stateTemp_1' : {
                        required : true
                    },

                    //cidade
                    'WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_city_1' : {
                        required : true
                    },
                    
                    

                        //sexo
                        'WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_FormInput_gender_In_Register_1' : {
                            required : true
                        },
    
                        //birth date
                        'WC_PersonalInfoExtension_birth_date, WC_PersonalInfoExtension_birth_month, WC_PersonalInfoExtension_birth_year' : {
                            multiDate : true
                        },
                    

                    //telefone
                    'WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_FormInput_phoneNum_In_Register_1' : {
                        required : true
                    },

                    //email
                    'WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_FormInput_email1_In_Register_1' : {
                        required : true,
                        email : true
                    },

                    //confirme email
                    'WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_FormInput_email_confirm' : {
                        required : true,
                        equalTo: 'WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_FormInput_email1_In_Register_1'
                    },					
		
                    //senha
                    'WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_FormInput_logonPassword_In_Register_1' : {
                        required : true
                    },

                    //confirme senha
                    'WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_FormInput_logonPasswordVerify_In_Register_1' : {
                        required : true,
                        equalTo: 'WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_FormInput_logonPassword_In_Register_1'
                    },
					
                    //SMS
                    'WC_PersonalInfoExtension_mobile_div_12' : {
                        required : dojo.byId('WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_FormInput_sendMeSMSPreference_In_Register_2').checked,
                        phone : dojo.byId('WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_FormInput_sendMeSMSPreference_In_Register_2').checked
                    }

                    
                },

                messages : {
                    
                            //nome
                            "WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_NameEntryForm_FormInput_firstName_1": {
                                required : 'Por favor, preencha o campo corretamente',

                            "WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_zipCode_1": {
                                required : 'Por favor, preencha o campo corretamente',
                                equalLen : 'Por favor, preencha o campo corretamente'
                            },
                        
                    
                    //logradouro
                    'WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_streetTypeTemp_1' : {
                        required : 'Por favor, selecione uma opção'
                    },

                    //endereco
                    'WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_address1_1' : {
                        required : 'Por favor, preencha o campo corretamente'
                    },

                    //numero
                    'WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_address2_1' : {
                        required : 'Por favor, preencha o campo corretamente'
                    },

                    //bairro
                    'WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_address2_3' : {
                        required : 'Por favor, preencha o campo corretamente'
                    },

                    //moradia
                    'WC_UserRegistrationAddForm_AddressEntryForm_FormInput_houseType_1' : {
                        required : 'Por favor, selecione uma opção'
